<h2><span id=".E4.BA.BA.E9.A1.9E.E5.88.A9.E7.94.A8"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="人类利用">人类利用</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="编辑章节：人类利用">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:S_cerevisiae_under_DIC_microscopy.jpg"><img alt="Microscopic view of five spherical structures; one of the spheres is considerably smaller than the rest and attached to one of the larger spheres" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1560" data-file-width="1560" decoding="async" height="170" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d9/S_cerevisiae_under_DIC_microscopy.jpg/170px-S_cerevisiae_under_DIC_microscopy.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d9/S_cerevisiae_under_DIC_microscopy.jpg/255px-S_cerevisiae_under_DIC_microscopy.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d9/S_cerevisiae_under_DIC_microscopy.jpg/340px-S_cerevisiae_under_DIC_microscopy.jpg 2x" width="170"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:S_cerevisiae_under_DIC_microscopy.jpg" title="放大"></a></div><a href="/wiki/%E5%BE%AE%E5%88%86%E5%B9%B2%E6%B6%89%E7%9B%B8%E5%B7%AE%E6%98%BE%E5%BE%AE%E9%95%9C" title="微分干涉相差显微镜">微分干涉相差显微镜</a>视野下的<a href="/wiki/%E9%87%80%E9%85%92%E9%85%B5%E6%AF%8D" title="酿酒酵母">酿酒酵母</a></div></div></div>
<p><span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Ethnomycology" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="人类真菌学"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%BA%BA%E9%A1%9E%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C%E5%AD%B8&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="人类真菌学（页面不存在）">人类真菌学</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ethnomycology" title="en:Ethnomycology"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Ethnomycology</span></a></span>）</span></span>是研究人类利用真菌的历史，以及真菌对人类社会影响的学门。长久以来，人类利用真菌来制造、保存食物，或用作其他用途。在许多国家<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Fungiculture" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="蕈类养殖"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%95%88%E9%A1%9E%E9%A4%8A%E6%AE%96&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="蕈类养殖（页面不存在）">蕈类养殖</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fungiculture" title="en:Fungiculture"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Fungiculture</span></a></span>）</span></span>与<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Mushroom hunting" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="蕈类采集"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%95%88%E9%A1%9E%E6%8E%A1%E9%9B%86&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="蕈类采集（页面不存在）">蕈类采集</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mushroom_hunting" title="en:Mushroom hunting"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Mushroom hunting</span></a></span>）</span></span>都是重要产业。因为许多真菌可以生产有生物活性的<a href="/wiki/%E5%A4%A9%E7%84%B6%E4%BA%A7%E7%89%A9" title="天然产物">天然产物</a>与抗生素，许多真菌已被开发、或正被开发以大量生产抗生素、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%B6%AD%E4%BB%96%E5%91%BD" title="维他命">维他命</a>、抗癌药物或降低<a href="/wiki/%E8%86%BD%E5%9B%BA%E9%86%87" title="胆固醇">胆固醇</a>的药物。近期随着在真菌进行<a href="/wiki/%E5%9F%BA%E5%9B%A0%E5%B7%A5%E7%A8%8B" title="基因工程">基因工程</a>的技术发展，使真菌的<a href="/wiki/%E4%BB%A3%E8%AC%9D%E5%B7%A5%E7%A8%8B%E5%AD%B8" title="代谢工程学">代谢工程</a>应用成为可能<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Finsham1989_205-0"><a href="#cite_note-Finsham1989-205">[199]</a></sup>。例如基因修饰后的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%85%B5%E6%AF%8D%E8%8F%8C" title="酵母菌">酵母菌</a>可以用来大量生产许多药物<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Hawkins2008_206-0"><a href="#cite_note-Hawkins2008-206">[200]</a></sup>，且因为酵母菌在培养箱中生长迅速，使生产药物的效率比从原本的来源提炼还要高<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Huang2008_207-0"><a href="#cite_note-Huang2008-207">[201]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E8.97.A5.E7.94.A8"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="药用">药用</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="编辑章节：药用">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id=".E7.95.B6.E4.BB.A3.E8.97.A5.E7.94.A8"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="当代药用">当代药用</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="编辑章节：当代药用">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%97%A5%E7%94%A8%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="药用真菌（页面不存在）">药用真菌</a></div>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Penicillium_notatum.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="615" data-file-width="640" decoding="async" height="211" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Penicillium_notatum.jpg/220px-Penicillium_notatum.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Penicillium_notatum.jpg/330px-Penicillium_notatum.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Penicillium_notatum.jpg/440px-Penicillium_notatum.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Penicillium_notatum.jpg" title="放大"></a></div><a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%A7%E9%BB%84%E9%9D%92%E9%9C%89%E8%8F%8C" title="产黄青霉菌">产黄青霉菌</a>可以合成<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%8B%84%E9%9D%92%E9%BB%B4%E7%B4%A0" title="苄青霉素">苄青霉素</a></div></div></div>
<p><br/>
许多真菌产生的代谢物可以作为药物。最着名的例子便是包括<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%9D%92%E9%BB%B4%E7%B4%A0" title="青霉素">青霉素</a>在内的<a href="/wiki/%E6%8A%97%E7%94%9F%E7%B4%A0" title="抗生素">抗生素</a>。在自然界中，真菌或细菌产生的抗生素通常有两种功用，一是高浓度时作为抑制其他微生物生长的抑制剂，以避免其他微生物与自己竞争资源，二是低浓度时作为物种内或物种间<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%BE%A4%E9%AB%94%E6%84%9F%E6%87%89" title="群体感应">群体感应</a>的讯息传递分子<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Fajardo2008_208-0"><a href="#cite_note-Fajardo2008-208">[202]</a></sup> 。自然界中产生的青霉素<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%8B%84%E9%9D%92%E9%BB%B4%E7%B4%A0" title="苄青霉素">苄青霉素</a>（由<a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%A7%E9%BB%84%E9%9D%92%E9%9C%89%E8%8F%8C" title="产黄青霉菌">产黄青霉菌</a>产生）可以有效杀死的细菌相对有限，但其他各式种类的青霉素可用<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%8C%96%E5%AD%B8%E5%90%88%E6%88%90" title="化学合成">化学方法</a>合成，以达到更广泛的杀菌能力，现代使用的青霉素便是<a href="/wiki/%E5%8D%8A%E5%90%88%E6%88%90" title="半合成">半合成</a>的产物，先由真菌合成，再针对需要的特殊性质对其进行化学修饰而得到最终产物<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Brakhage2004_209-0"><a href="#cite_note-Brakhage2004-209">[203]</a></sup>。除了青霉素外，由真菌生产的抗生素还包括<a href="/wiki/%E7%8E%AF%E5%AD%A2%E7%B4%A0" title="环孢素">环孢素</a>（在<a href="/wiki/%E5%99%A8%E5%AE%98%E7%A7%BB%E6%A4%8D" title="器官移植">器官移植</a>时用作<a href="/wiki/%E5%85%8D%E7%96%AB%E6%8A%91%E5%88%B6%E5%8A%91" title="免疫抑制剂">免疫抑制剂</a>）、<a href="/wiki/%E5%A4%AB%E8%A5%BF%E5%9C%B0%E9%85%B8" title="夫西地酸">夫西地酸</a>（可用来处理<a href="/wiki/%E8%80%90%E7%94%B2%E6%B0%A7%E8%A5%BF%E6%9E%97%E9%87%91%E9%BB%84%E8%89%B2%E8%91%A1%E8%90%84%E7%90%83%E8%8F%8C" title="耐甲氧西林金黄色葡萄球菌">耐甲氧西林金黄色葡萄球菌</a>的感染<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Pan2008_210-0"><a href="#cite_note-Pan2008-210">[204]</a></sup> ）与<a href="/wiki/%E7%81%B0%E9%BB%83%E9%BB%B4%E7%B4%A0" title="灰黄霉素">灰黄霉素</a>（可治疗<a href="/wiki/%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C%E7%97%85" title="真菌病">真菌感染</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Loo2006_211-0"><a href="#cite_note-Loo2006-211">[205]</a></sup>）。
另外，可以抑制<a href="/wiki/%E7%BE%9F%E7%94%B2%E5%9F%BA%E6%88%8A%E4%BA%8C%E9%85%B8%E5%8D%95%E9%85%B0%E8%BE%85%E9%85%B6A%E8%BF%98%E5%8E%9F%E9%85%B6" title="羟甲基戊二酸单酰辅酶A还原酶">羟甲基戊二酸单醯辅酶A还原酶</a>，继而抑制<a href="/wiki/%E8%86%BD%E5%9B%BA%E9%86%87" title="胆固醇">胆固醇</a>合成的<a href="/wiki/%E4%BB%96%E6%B1%80" title="他汀">他汀</a>类药物，许多也是由真菌合成的，例如由<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Penicillium citrinum" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="橘青霉"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%A9%98%E9%9D%92%E9%BB%B4&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="橘青霉（页面不存在）">橘青霉</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Penicillium_citrinum" title="en:Penicillium citrinum"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Penicillium citrinum</span></a></span>）</span></span>合成的<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Mevastatin" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="美伐他汀"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BE%8E%E4%BC%90%E4%BB%96%E6%B1%80&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="美伐他汀（页面不存在）">美伐他汀</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mevastatin" title="en:Mevastatin"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Mevastatin</span></a></span>）</span></span>，以及由<a href="/wiki/%E5%9C%9F%E9%BA%B4%E9%BB%B4" title="土麴霉">土麴霉</a>与<a href="/wiki/%E5%B9%B3%E8%8F%87" title="平菇">平菇</a>合成的<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Lovastatin" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="洛伐他汀"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%B4%9B%E4%BC%90%E4%BB%96%E6%B1%80&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="洛伐他汀（页面不存在）">洛伐他汀</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lovastatin" title="en:Lovastatin"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Lovastatin</span></a></span>）</span></span><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Manzoni2002_212-0"><a href="#cite_note-Manzoni2002-212">[206]</a></sup>。真菌也能生产抑制<a href="/wiki/%E7%97%85%E6%AF%92" title="病毒">病毒</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-elMekkawy1998_213-0"><a href="#cite_note-elMekkawy1998-213">[207]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ElDine2008_214-0"><a href="#cite_note-ElDine2008-214">[208]</a></sup>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%99%8C%E7%B4%B0%E8%83%9E" title="癌细胞">癌细胞</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Hetland2008_215-0"><a href="#cite_note-Hetland2008-215">[209]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Yuen2005_216-0"><a href="#cite_note-Yuen2005-216">[210]</a></sup>生长的药物，例如产于<a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%B2%E8%8A%9D" title="云芝">云芝</a>的抗癌药物<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Polysaccharide-K" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="云芝多糖K"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%B2%E8%8A%9D%E5%A4%9A%E9%86%A3K&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="云芝多糖K（页面不存在）">云芝多糖K</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polysaccharide-K" title="en:Polysaccharide-K"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Polysaccharide-K</span></a></span>）</span></span>已在欧洲与日本等地作为抗癌药物的<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Adjuvant" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="佐剂"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%BD%90%E5%8A%91&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="佐剂（页面不存在）">佐剂</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Adjuvant" title="en:Adjuvant"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Adjuvant</span></a></span>）</span></span>使用<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Fisher2002_217-0"><a href="#cite_note-Fisher2002-217">[211]</a></sup>，产于<a href="/wiki/%E9%A6%99%E8%8F%87" title="香菇">香菇</a>的<a href="/wiki/%E9%A6%99%E8%8F%87%E5%A4%9A%E7%B3%96" title="香菇多糖">香菇多糖</a>也在日本等国被用在癌症治疗中<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Sullivan2006_218-0"><a href="#cite_note-Sullivan2006-218">[212]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Halpern2002_219-0"><a href="#cite_note-Halpern2002-219">[213]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h4><span id=".E5.82.B3.E7.B5.B1.E9.86.AB.E5.AD.B8"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="传统医学">传统医学</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="编辑章节：传统医学">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>

style="width:182px;max-width:182px"><div class="thumbimage"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:CordycepsSinensis.jpg"><img alt="Two dried yellow-orange caterpillars, one with a curly grayish fungus growing out of one of its ends. The grayish fungus is roughly equal to or slightly greater in length than the caterpillar, and tapers in thickness to a narrow end." data-file-height="1136" data-file-width="1948" decoding="async" height="105" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/94/CordycepsSinensis.jpg/180px-CordycepsSinensis.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/94/CordycepsSinensis.jpg/270px-CordycepsSinensis.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/94/CordycepsSinensis.jpg/360px-CordycepsSinensis.jpg 2x" width="180"/></a></div></div></div><div class="trow" style="display:flex"><div class="thumbcaption">两种中医常用的药用真菌：<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%B5%A4%E8%8A%9D&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="赤芝（页面不存在）">赤芝</a>（左）与<a href="/wiki/%E5%86%AC%E8%99%AB%E5%A4%8F%E8%8D%89" title="冬虫夏草">冬虫夏草</a>（右）</div></div></div></div>
<p>许多真菌是<a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%AD%E5%8C%BB%E5%AD%A6" title="中医学">中医</a>等<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%82%B3%E7%B5%B1%E9%86%AB%E5%AD%B8" title="传统医学">传统医学</a>使用的药材，中医用来入药的真菌包括<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%A7%AC%E6%9D%BE%E8%8C%B8" title="姬松茸">姬松茸</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Hetland2008_215-1"><a href="#cite_note-Hetland2008-215">[209]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Firenzuoli2008_220-0"><a href="#cite_note-Firenzuoli2008-220">[214]</a></sup>、<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%B5%A4%E8%8A%9D&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="赤芝（页面不存在）">赤芝</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Paterson2006_221-0"><a href="#cite_note-Paterson2006-221">[215]</a></sup>与<a href="/wiki/%E5%86%AC%E8%99%AB%E5%A4%8F%E8%8D%89" title="冬虫夏草">冬虫夏草</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Paterson2008_222-0"><a href="#cite_note-Paterson2008-222">[216]</a></sup>等。冬虫夏草是<a href="/wiki/%E5%AD%90%E5%9B%8A%E8%8F%8C%E9%97%A8" title="子囊菌门">子囊菌门</a>的真菌中华虫草寄生于<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Hepialidae" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="蝙蝠蛾"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%9D%99%E8%9D%A0%E8%9B%BE&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="蝙蝠蛾（页面不存在）">蝙蝠蛾</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hepialidae" title="en:Hepialidae"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Hepialidae</span></a></span>）</span></span>幼虫后，死亡的幼虫与菌丝所组成。最早将冬虫夏草入药的地方是<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%A5%BF%E8%97%8F" title="西藏">西藏</a>与<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%B0%BC%E6%B3%8A%E7%88%BE" title="尼泊尔">尼泊尔</a>，十五世纪的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%97%8F%E9%86%AB" title="藏医">藏医</a>医生舒卡·年姆多吉（Zurkhar Nyamnyi Dorje）在其着作《药方汇集》中提到冬虫夏草，是冬虫夏草用于传统医学的最早文字纪录<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Winkler2008b_223-0"><a href="#cite_note-Winkler2008b-223">[217]</a></sup>。中国对冬虫夏草最早的记载是<a href="/wiki/%E6%B8%85%E6%9C%9D" title="清朝">清朝</a><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%B1%AA%E6%98%82&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="汪昂（页面不存在）">汪昂</a>在《本草备要》一书中所写「冬虫夏草，甘平，保肺益肾，止血化痰，止劳咳。四川嘉定府所产者佳。冬在土中，形如老蚕，有毛能动，至夏则毛出土上，连身俱化为草。若不取，至冬复化为虫。」<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Winkler2008_224-0"><a href="#cite_note-Winkler2008-224">[218]</a></sup>中医认为冬虫夏草是名贵滋补的草药，有「甘平保肺，益肾止血，化痰，已劳嗽」之效<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-225"><a href="#cite_note-225">[219]</a></sup>。
</p><p>属于<a href="/wiki/%E6%8B%85%E5%AD%90%E8%8F%8C%E9%97%A8" title="担子菌门">担子菌门</a>的<a href="/wiki/%E6%A1%91%E9%BB%83" title="桑黄">桑黄</a>是另一种传统医学使用的草药，<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%B8%AD%E9%86%AB" title="中医">中医</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%9F%93%E9%86%AB" title="韩医">韩医</a>与<a href="/wiki/%E6%97%A5%E6%9C%AC%E6%BC%A2%E6%96%B9%E9%86%AB%E5%AD%B8" title="日本汉方医学">日本汉方医学</a>皆有使用纪录。早在秦汉时的《<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%A5%9E%E8%BE%B2%E6%9C%AC%E8%8D%89%E7%B6%93" title="神农本草经">神农本草经</a>》就有桑黄入药的纪录，中医认为桑黄有止血与治疗妇女病的功效，<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%9C%9D%E9%B2%9C%E6%97%B6%E4%BB%A3" title="朝鲜时代">朝鲜时代</a>的医书《<a href="/wiki/%E4%B9%A1%E8%8D%AF%E9%9B%86%E6%88%90%E6%96%B9" title="乡药集成方">乡药集成方</a>》与《<a href="/wiki/%E6%9D%B1%E9%86%AB%E5%AF%B6%E9%91%91" title="东医宝鉴">东医宝鉴</a>》均记载桑黄有如灵丹妙药，<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%B1%9F%E6%88%B6%E6%99%82%E4%BB%A3" title="江户时代">江户时代</a>的<a href="/wiki/%E6%97%A5%E6%9C%AC" title="日本">日本</a>也将桑黄当作汉方药<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-226"><a href="#cite_note-226">[220]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E9.A3.9F.E7.94.A8"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="食用">食用</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="编辑章节：食用">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Asian_mushrooms.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="564" data-file-width="1024" decoding="async" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f8/Asian_mushrooms.jpg/300px-Asian_mushrooms.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f8/Asian_mushrooms.jpg/450px-Asian_mushrooms.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f8/Asian_mushrooms.jpg/600px-Asian_mushrooms.jpg 2x" width="300"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Asian_mushrooms.jpg" title="放大"></a></div>一些亚洲常见的<a href="/wiki/%E9%A3%9F%E7%94%A8%E8%95%88" title="食用蕈">食用蕈</a></div></div></div>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a href="/wiki/%E9%A3%9F%E7%94%A8%E8%95%88" title="食用蕈">食用蕈</a></div>
<p><a href="/wiki/%E9%A3%9F%E7%94%A8%E8%95%88" title="食用蕈">食用蕈</a>有些是野外采集的，有些则是商业种植的。西方最常食用的蕈类是<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%B4%8B%E8%8F%87" title="洋菇">洋菇</a>，用在沙拉、汤品与许多其他料理中。许多在亚洲常被种植、食用的蕈类，例如<a href="/wiki/%E8%8D%89%E8%8F%87" title="草菇">草菇</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E5%B9%B3%E8%8F%87" title="平菇">平菇</a>与<a href="/wiki/%E9%87%91%E9%87%9D%E8%8F%87" title="金针菇">金针菇</a>也渐渐传到西方<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Stamets2000_227-0"><a href="#cite_note-Stamets2000-227">[221]</a></sup>。许多其他种蕈类可由野外采集来食用或贩卖，包括<a href="/wiki/%E6%9D%BE%E4%B9%B3%E8%8F%87" title="松乳菇">松乳菇</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%BE%8A%E8%82%9A%E8%8F%8C" title="羊肚菌">羊肚菌</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E9%B8%A1%E6%B2%B9%E8%8F%87" title="鸡油菇">鸡油菇</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E6%9D%BE%E9%9C%B2" title="松露">松露</a>、<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Craterellus" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="喇叭菌"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%96%87%E5%8F%AD%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="喇叭菌（页面不存在）">喇叭菌</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Craterellus" title="en:Craterellus"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Craterellus</span></a></span>）</span></span>与<a href="/wiki/%E7%BE%8E%E5%91%B3%E7%89%9B%E8%82%9D%E8%8F%8C" title="美味牛肝菌">美味牛肝菌</a>等，有些种类在市场上的价格十分高昂，通常是特殊料理中的食材<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-228"><a href="#cite_note-228">[222]</a></sup>。
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Blue_Stilton_Quarter_Front.jpg"><img alt="A corner of cheese with greenish streaks through it" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="700" data-file-width="903" decoding="async" height="171" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d3/Blue_Stilton_Quarter_Front.jpg/220px-Blue_Stilton_Quarter_Front.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d3/Blue_Stilton_Quarter_Front.jpg/330px-Blue_Stilton_Quarter_Front.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d3/Blue_Stilton_Quarter_Front.jpg/440px-Blue_Stilton_Quarter_Front.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Blue_Stilton_Quarter_Front.jpg" title="放大"></a></div><span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Penicillium roqueforti" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="罗克福青霉菌"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BE%85%E5%85%8B%E7%A6%8F%E9%9D%92%E9%BB%B4%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="罗克福青霉菌（页面不存在）">罗克福青霉菌</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Penicillium_roqueforti" title="en:Penicillium roqueforti"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Penicillium roqueforti</span></a></span>）</span></span>产生<a href="/wiki/%E6%96%AF%E8%92%82%E7%88%BE%E9%A0%93%E8%8A%9D%E5%A3%AB" title="斯蒂尔顿芝士">斯蒂尔顿芝士</a>上的蓝绿色花纹</div></div></div>
<p>生产某些种<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%B5%B7%E5%8F%B8" title="起司">起司</a>时需要把特定真菌加到<a href="/wiki/%E5%87%9D%E4%B9%B3" title="凝乳">凝乳</a>中，以产生特殊的风味或口感，例如<a href="/wiki/%E6%96%AF%E8%92%82%E7%88%BE%E9%A0%93%E8%8A%9D%E5%A3%AB" title="斯蒂尔顿芝士">斯蒂尔顿芝士</a>与<a href="/wiki/%E7%BD%97%E5%85%8B%E7%A6%8F%E5%B9%B2%E9%85%AA" title="罗克福干酪">罗克福干酪</a>上的蓝色纹路便是<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Penicillium roqueforti" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="罗克福青霉菌"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BE%85%E5%85%8B%E7%A6%8F%E9%9D%92%E9%BB%B4%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="罗克福青霉菌（页面不存在）">罗克福青霉菌</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Penicillium_roqueforti" title="en:Penicillium roqueforti"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Penicillium roqueforti</span></a></span>）</span></span>造成的<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Kinsella1976_229-0"><a href="#cite_note-Kinsella1976-229">[223]</a></sup>。用于制造起司的真菌都是无毒的，但起司成熟或贮藏时，可能有其他种类的真菌生长于其上，而产生多种<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="mycotoxin" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="真菌毒素"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C%E6%AF%92%E7%B4%A0&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="真菌毒素（页面不存在）">真菌毒素</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/mycotoxin" title="en:mycotoxin"><span dir="auto" lang="en">mycotoxin</span></a></span>）</span></span>，是生产起司时需考虑的因素<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Erdogan2004_230-0"><a href="#cite_note-Erdogan2004-230">[224]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h4><span id=".E7.99.BC.E9.85.B5.E9.A3.9F.E5.93.81"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="发酵食品">发酵食品</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="编辑章节：发酵食品">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><a href="/wiki/%E9%87%80%E9%85%92%E9%85%B5%E6%AF%8D" title="酿酒酵母">酿酒酵母</a>常用来制作<a href="/wiki/%E9%BA%B5%E5%8C%85" title="面包">面包</a>与其他小麦加工食品<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Kulp2000_231-0"><a href="#cite_note-Kulp2000-231">[225]</a></sup>，许多酵母菌可用来<a href="/wiki/%E9%85%BF%E9%85%92" title="酿酒">酿酒</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Piskur2006_232-0"><a href="#cite_note-Piskur2006-232">[226]</a></sup>，<a href="/wiki/%E7%B1%B3%E9%BA%B4%E8%8F%8C" title="米麴菌">米麴菌</a>则可用来发酵大豆，制作<a href="/wiki/%E9%85%B1%E6%B2%B9" title="酱油">酱油</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E6%97%A5%E6%9C%AC%E9%85%92" title="日本酒">日本酒</a>与<a href="/wiki/%E5%91%B3%E5%99%8C" title="味噌">味噌</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Abe2006_233-0"><a href="#cite_note-Abe2006-233">[227]</a></sup>，<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%A0%B9%E9%9C%89" title="根霉">根霉</a>则是制作印尼食品<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%B8%B9%E8%B2%9D" title="丹贝">丹贝</a>的重要原料<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Hachmeister1993_234-0"><a href="#cite_note-Hachmeister1993-234">[228]</a></sup>。许多与这些真菌亲缘相当接近的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%BA%B4%E8%8F%8C%E5%B1%AC" title="麴菌属">麴菌属</a>真菌会产生对人体有害的毒素，但这些真菌大多是<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%A6%B4%E5%8C%96" title="驯化">驯化物种</a>，经由育种、人择选出发酵能力佳，又不会产生<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="mycotoxin" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="真菌毒素"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C%E6%AF%92%E7%B4%A0&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="真菌毒素（页面不存在）">真菌毒素</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/mycotoxin" title="en:mycotoxin"><span dir="auto" lang="en">mycotoxin</span></a></span>）</span></span>的真菌种类用于食品工业中<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Jorgensen2007_235-0"><a href="#cite_note-Jorgensen2007-235">[229]</a></sup> 。另外<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Quorn" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="阔恩牌素肉"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%97%8A%E6%81%A9%E7%89%8C%E7%B4%A0%E8%82%89&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="阔恩牌素肉（页面不存在）">阔恩牌素肉</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Quorn" title="en:Quorn"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Quorn</span></a></span>）</span></span>也是真菌衍生的食品，由<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Fusarium venenatum" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="金黄色镰孢"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%87%91%E9%BB%83%E8%89%B2%E9%90%AE%E5%AD%A2&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="金黄色镰孢（页面不存在）">金黄色镰孢</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fusarium_venenatum" title="en:Fusarium venenatum"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Fusarium venenatum</span></a></span>）</span></span>发酵而成<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ODonnell1998_236-0"><a href="#cite_note-ODonnell1998-236">[230]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E6.9C.89.E6.AF.92.E7.9C.9F.E8.8F.8C"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="有毒真菌">有毒真菌</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;section=39" title="编辑章节：有毒真菌">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Amanita_phalloides_1.JPG"><img alt="Two light yellow-green mushrooms with stems and caps, one smaller and still in the ground, the larger one pulled out and laid beside the other to show its bulbous stem with a ring" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1600" data-file-width="1200" decoding="async" height="227" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/99/Amanita_phalloides_1.JPG/170px-Amanita_phalloides_1.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/99/Amanita_phalloides_1.JPG/255px-Amanita_phalloides_1.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/99/Amanita_phalloides_1.JPG/340px-Amanita_phalloides_1.JPG 2x" width="170"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Amanita_phalloides_1.JPG" title="放大"></a></div><a href="/wiki/%E6%AF%92%E9%B5%9D%E8%86%8F" title="毒鹅膏">毒鹅膏</a>造成了全世界超过一半<a href="/wiki/%E8%95%88%E9%A1%9E%E4%B8%AD%E6%AF%92" title="蕈类中毒">蕈类中毒</a>造成的死亡</div></div></div>
<p>许多真菌对人类是有毒的，毒性可轻至造成肠胃不适或过敏，重至产生幻觉、器官衰竭甚至致死。有毒的蕈类包括<a href="/wiki/%E9%94%A5%E7%9B%96%E4%BC%9E%E5%B1%9E" title="锥盖伞属">锥盖伞属</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E7%9B%94%E5%AD%A2%E4%BC%9E%E5%B1%9E" title="盔孢伞属">盔孢伞属</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E7%8E%AF%E6%9F%84%E8%8F%87%E5%B1%9E" title="环柄菇属">环柄菇属</a>与最恶名昭彰的<a href="/wiki/%E9%B5%9D%E8%86%8F%E8%8F%8C%E5%B1%AC" title="鹅膏菌属">鹅膏菌属</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Orr1979_237-0"><a href="#cite_note-Orr1979-237">[231]</a></sup>，鹅膏菌属包含号称毁灭天使的<a href="/wiki/%E9%B1%97%E6%9F%84%E7%99%BD%E9%B5%9D%E8%86%8F" title="鳞柄白鹅膏">鳞柄白鹅膏</a>与<a href="/wiki/%E6%AF%92%E9%B5%9D%E8%86%8F" title="毒鹅膏">毒鹅膏</a>，后者常被误认成可食用的<a href="/wiki/%E8%8D%89%E8%8F%87" title="草菇">草菇</a>而误食致死，占人类因毒菇中毒死亡的比例超过半数<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Vetter1998_238-0"><a href="#cite_note-Vetter1998-238">[232]</a></sup> 。<a href="/wiki/%E9%B9%BF%E8%8A%B1%E8%8F%8C" title="鹿花菌">鹿花菌</a>煮熟后一般可以食用，且被许多人视为美食，但生食则有剧毒<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Leathem2007_239-0"><a href="#cite_note-Leathem2007-239">[233]</a></sup>，<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Tricholoma equestre" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="油口蘑"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%B2%B9%E5%8F%A3%E8%98%91&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="油口蘑（页面不存在）">油口蘑</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tricholoma_equestre" title="en:Tricholoma equestre"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Tricholoma equestre</span></a></span>）</span></span>甚至在<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%B8%AD%E4%B8%96%E7%B4%80" title="中世纪">中世纪</a>长期被认为可以食用，且受到某些<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%A8%8E%E5%A3%AB" title="骑士">骑士</a>的喜爱，后来才发现这种蕈类有剧毒，会导致<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%A9%AB%E7%B4%8B%E8%82%8C%E6%BA%B6%E8%A7%A3%E7%97%87" title="横纹肌溶解症">横纹肌溶解症</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-KarlsonStiber2003_240-0"><a href="#cite_note-KarlsonStiber2003-240">[234]</a></sup>。<a href="/wiki/%E6%AF%92%E8%A0%85%E5%82%98" title="毒蝇伞">毒蝇伞</a>也常造成不致死的中毒，多半是当<a href="/wiki/%E8%87%B4%E5%B9%BB%E5%89%82" title="致幻剂">致幻剂</a>吸食所造成，历史上毒蝇伞曾被欧洲与亚洲的许多人群拿来吸食，直到现在仍被<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%A7%91%E9%87%8C%E4%BA%9E%E5%85%8B%E6%97%8F" title="科里亚克族">科里亚克族</a>等<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%A5%BF%E4%BC%AF%E5%88%A9%E4%BA%9E" title="西伯利亚">西伯利亚</a>东北部的民族在<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%96%A9%E6%BB%BF%E6%95%99" title="萨满教">萨满教</a>仪式上用做致幻性药品<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Michelot2003_241-0"><a href="#cite_note-Michelot2003-241">[235]</a></sup>。
</p><p>未受专业训练的人很难正确分辨蕈类是否可食，因此专家通常建议将所有在野外发现的蕈类视为有毒的，不要食用<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-242"><a href="#cite_note-242">[236]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Ammirati1987_243-0"><a href="#cite_note-Ammirati1987-243">[237]</a></sup>。若误食毒菇出现症状，应保留剩下的菇与呕吐物等检体并立即就医<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-244"><a href="#cite_note-244">[238]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E8.9F.B2.E5.AE.B3.E7.AE.A1.E7.90.86"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="虫害管理">虫害管理</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;section=40" title="编辑章节：虫害管理">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Beauveria.jpg"><img alt="Two dead grasshoppers with a whitish fuzz growing on them" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1166" data-file-width="1200" decoding="async" height="214" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c3/Beauveria.jpg/220px-Beauveria.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c3/Beauveria.jpg/330px-Beauveria.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c3/Beauveria.jpg/440px-Beauveria.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Beauveria.jpg" title="放大"></a></div>被<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Beauveria bassiana" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="巴氏蚕白僵菌"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%B7%B4%E6%B0%8F%E8%A0%B6%E7%99%BD%E5%83%B5%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="巴氏蚕白僵菌（页面不存在）">巴氏蚕白僵菌</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Beauveria_bassiana" title="en:Beauveria bassiana"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Beauveria bassiana</span></a></span>）</span></span>杀死的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%9A%B1%E8%9C%A2" title="蚱蜢">蚱蜢</a></div></div></div>
<p>在农业上，根据<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%AB%B6%E7%88%AD%E6%8E%92%E9%99%A4%E5%8E%9F%E5%89%87" title="竞争排除原则">竞争排除原则</a>，真菌若可以与有害的细菌或其他真菌竞争资源与空间，甚至寄生这些微生物，抑制有害菌，都可用作<a href="/wiki/%E7%94%9F%E7%89%A9%E9%98%B2%E6%B2%BB" title="生物防治">生物防治</a>以减少病虫害<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-LopezGomez2006_245-0"><a href="#cite_note-LopezGomez2006-245">[239]</a></sup>。许多真菌可抑制<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%9F%8E" title="蟎">蟎</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E6%9D%82%E8%8D%89" title="杂草">杂草</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%BA%BF%E8%99%AB" title="线虫">线虫</a>或其他有害于作物的真菌生长<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-urlUSDA_Biocontrol_246-0"><a href="#cite_note-urlUSDA_Biocontrol-246">[240]</a></sup>，在生物防治上产生了许多应用。<a href="/wiki/%E8%99%AB%E7%94%9F%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C" title="虫生真菌">虫生真菌</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-urlwww.uvminnovations.com_247-0"><a href="#cite_note-urlwww.uvminnovations.com-247">[241]</a></sup>如<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Beauveria bassiana" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="白僵菌"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%99%BD%E5%83%B5%E8%8F%8C" title="白僵菌">白僵菌</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Beauveria_bassiana" title="en:Beauveria bassiana"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Beauveria bassiana</span></a></span>）</span></span>、<a href="/wiki/%E9%BB%91%E6%AE%AD%E8%8F%8C" title="黑僵菌">黑僵菌</a>、<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Hirsutella" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="被毛孢"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%A2%AB%E6%AF%9B%E5%AD%A2&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="被毛孢（页面不存在）">被毛孢</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hirsutella" title="en:Hirsutella"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Hirsutella</span></a></span>）</span></span>、<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Paecilomyces" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="拟青霉菌"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%93%AC%E9%9D%92%E9%BB%B4%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="拟青霉菌（页面不存在）">拟青霉菌</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Paecilomyces" title="en:Paecilomyces"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Paecilomyces</span></a></span>）</span></span>与<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Lecanicillium lecanii" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="蜡蚧轮枝菌"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%A0%9F%E8%9A%A7%E8%BC%AA%E6%9E%9D%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="蜡蚧轮枝菌（页面不存在）">蜡蚧轮枝菌</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lecanicillium_lecanii" title="en:Lecanicillium lecanii"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Lecanicillium lecanii</span></a></span>）</span></span>等皆可抑制害虫生长而用作<a href="/wiki/%E7%94%9F%E7%89%A9%E8%BE%B2%E8%97%A5" title="生物农药">生物农药</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Deshpande1999_248-0"><a href="#cite_note-Deshpande1999-248">[242]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Thomas2007_249-0"><a href="#cite_note-Thomas2007-249">[243]</a></sup>。<i>Neotyphodium</i>、<a href="/wiki/%E9%A6%99%E6%9F%B1%E8%8F%8C%E5%B1%9E" title="香柱菌属">香柱菌属</a>等内生真菌生长在植物体内，可以合成<a href="/wiki/%E7%94%9F%E7%89%A9%E9%B9%BC" title="生物碱">生物碱</a>以避免植物受到<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%8D%89%E9%A3%9F%E5%8B%95%E7%89%A9" title="草食动物">草食动物</a>啃食<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Bush1997_250-0"><a href="#cite_note-Bush1997-250">[244]</a></sup>，这种特性也被人利用在<a href="/wiki/%E6%94%BE%E7%89%A7%E5%A0%B4" title="放牧场">放牧场</a>等草地的栽培中，经由<a href="/wiki/%E6%A4%8D%E7%89%A9%E9%85%8D%E7%A8%AE" title="植物配种">植物配种</a>选择分泌物只对昆虫有毒性，而对家畜无害真菌<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Bouton2002_251-0"><a href="#cite_note-Bouton2002-251">[245]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E7.9C.9F.E8.8F.8C.E4.BF.AE.E5.BE.A9"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="真菌修复">真菌修复</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;section=41" title="编辑章节：真菌修复">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a href="/wiki/%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C%E4%BF%AE%E5%BE%A9" title="真菌修复">真菌修复</a></div>
<p>真菌修复是<a href="/wiki/%E7%94%9F%E7%89%A9%E4%BF%AE%E5%BE%A9" title="生物修复">生物修复</a>的一种，意指以真菌来降解环境中的污染物。已知某些真菌可以将<a href="/wiki/%E6%AE%BA%E8%9F%B2%E5%8A%91" title="杀虫剂">杀虫剂</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%99%A4%E8%8D%89%E5%8A%91" title="除草剂">除草剂</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%B6%88%E6%AF%92%E5%8A%91" title="消毒剂">消毒剂</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E7%9F%BF%E7%89%A9%E6%9D%82%E9%85%9A%E6%B2%B9" title="矿物杂酚油">矿物杂酚油</a>、甚至长链石油分解成二氧化碳与水<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Christian2005_252-0"><a href="#cite_note-Christian2005-252">[246]</a></sup>，还可以吸收环境中的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%87%8D%E9%87%91%E5%B1%AC" title="重金属">重金属</a>并储存于子实体中。有些真菌甚至能用来清理受<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%A0%B8%E6%B1%A1%E6%9F%93" title="核污染">核污染</a>的土地，<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BBC2008_253-0"><a href="#cite_note-BBC2008-253">[247]</a></sup>核废料中的<a href="/wiki/%E8%B2%A7%E9%88%BE" title="贫铀">贫铀</a>在环境中容易被氧化，而铀氧化物可以被植物与细菌所吸收，在食物链中层层累积。真菌可以经由<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Biomineralization" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="生物矿化作用"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%94%9F%E7%89%A9%E7%A4%A6%E5%8C%96%E4%BD%9C%E7%94%A8&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="生物矿化作用（页面不存在）">生物矿化作用</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Biomineralization" title="en:Biomineralization"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Biomineralization</span></a></span>）</span></span>将铀氧化物固定成磷酸盐矿物，这种型式的铀不易被生物所吸收，不会进入食物链中对生物造成危害<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Fomina2007_254-0"><a href="#cite_note-Fomina2007-254">[248]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Fomina2008_255-0"><a href="#cite_note-Fomina2008-255">[249]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E6.A8.A1.E5.BC.8F.E7.94.9F.E7.89.A9"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="模式生物">模式生物</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;section=42" title="编辑章节：模式生物">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>许多生物学上的重大发现都得益于将真菌用作<a href="/wiki/%E6%A8%A1%E5%BC%8F%E7%94%9F%E7%89%A9" title="模式生物">模式生物</a>的研究，例如<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="One gene–one enzyme hypothesis" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="一基因一酵素假说"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%B8%80%E5%9F%BA%E5%9B%A0%E4%B8%80%E9%85%B5%E7%B4%A0%E5%81%87%E8%AA%AA&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="一基因一酵素假说（页面不存在）">一基因一酵素假说</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/One_gene%E2%80%93one_enzyme_hypothesis" title="en:One gene–one enzyme hypothesis"><span dir="auto" lang="en">One gene–one enzyme hypothesis</span></a></span>）</span></span>便是用<a href="/wiki/%E7%B2%89%E8%89%B2%E9%BA%B5%E5%8C%85%E9%BB%B4%E8%8F%8C" title="粉色面包霉菌">粉色面包霉菌</a>的实验证实的<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Beadle1941_256-0"><a href="#cite_note-Beadle1941-256">[250]</a></sup>。<a href="/wiki/%E9%87%80%E9%85%92%E9%85%B5%E6%AF%8D" title="酿酒酵母">酿酒酵母</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%A3%82%E6%AE%96%E9%85%B5%E6%AF%8D" title="裂殖酵母">裂殖酵母</a>与<a href="/wiki/%E5%B0%8F%E5%B7%A2%E7%8B%80%E9%BA%B4%E8%8F%8C" title="小巢状麴菌">小巢状麴菌</a>也都是重要的模式生物，长久以来用于有关<a href="/wiki/%E7%B4%B0%E8%83%9E%E9%80%B1%E6%9C%9F" title="细胞周期">细胞周期</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%9F%93%E8%89%B2%E9%AB%94" title="染色体">染色体</a>结构与<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Regulation of gene expression" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="基因表现调控"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9F%BA%E5%9B%A0%E8%A1%A8%E7%8F%BE%E8%AA%BF%E6%8E%A7&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="基因表现调控（页面不存在）">基因表现调控</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Regulation_of_gene_expression" title="en:Regulation of gene expression"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Regulation of gene expression</span></a></span>）</span></span>等<a href="/wiki/%E7%9C%9F%E6%A0%B8%E7%94%9F%E7%89%A9" title="真核生物">真核生物</a><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%81%BA%E5%82%B3%E5%AD%B8" title="遗传学">遗传学</a>与<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%B4%B0%E8%83%9E%E7%94%9F%E7%89%A9%E5%AD%B8" title="细胞生物学">细胞生物学</a>的基础研究。近年来有更多真菌被当成医学、植物病理与工业研究的模式生物，例如人类的病原菌<a href="/wiki/%E7%99%BD%E8%89%B2%E5%BF%B5%E7%8F%A0%E8%8F%8C" title="白色念珠菌">白色念珠菌</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Datta1989_257-0"><a href="#cite_note-Datta1989-257">[251]</a></sup>、植物病原菌<a href="/wiki/%E7%A8%BB%E7%86%B1%E7%97%85%E8%8F%8C" title="稻热病菌">稻热病菌</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Dean2005_258-0"><a href="#cite_note-Dean2005-258">[252]</a></sup>与工业上常用来大量生产真核生物蛋白质的<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Pichia pastoris" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="嗜甲醇酵母菌"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%97%9C%E7%94%B2%E9%86%87%E9%85%B5%E6%AF%8D%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="嗜甲醇酵母菌（页面不存在）">嗜甲醇酵母菌</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pichia_pastoris" title="en:Pichia pastoris"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Pichia pastoris</span></a></span>）</span></span><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Daly2005_259-0"><a href="#cite_note-Daly2005-259">[253]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E5.85.B6.E4.BB.96"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="其他">其他</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;section=43" title="编辑章节：其他">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>真菌被广泛用来生产<a href="/wiki/%E6%AA%B8%E6%AA%AC%E9%85%B8" title="柠檬酸">柠檬酸</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E8%91%A1%E8%90%84%E7%B3%96%E9%85%B8" title="葡萄糖酸">葡萄糖酸</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E4%B9%B3%E9%85%B8" title="乳酸">乳酸</a>与<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%98%8B%E6%9E%9C%E9%85%B8" title="苹果酸">苹果酸</a>等化学物质<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Schlegel1993_260-0"><a href="#cite_note-Schlegel1993-260">[254]</a></sup> ，以及工业用的酵素，例如<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%B4%97%E8%A1%A3%E7%B2%89" title="洗衣粉">洗衣粉</a>里的<a href="/wiki/%E8%84%82%E9%85%B6" title="脂酶">脂酶</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Joseph2008_261-0"><a href="#cite_note-Joseph2008-261">[255]</a></sup>、用来生产<a href="/wiki/%E7%BA%96%E7%B6%AD%E7%B4%A0%E4%B9%99%E9%86%87" title="纤维素乙醇">纤维素乙醇</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Kumar2008_262-0"><a href="#cite_note-Kumar2008-262">[256]</a></sup>和<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%89%9B%E4%BB%94%E8%A4%B2" title="牛仔裤">牛仔裤</a><span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Stone washing" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="酵素石洗"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%85%B5%E7%B4%A0%E7%9F%B3%E6%B4%97&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="酵素石洗（页面不存在）">酵素石洗</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Stone_washing" title="en:Stone washing"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Stone washing</span></a></span>）</span></span><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nysaes_263-0"><a href="#cite_note-nysaes-263">[257]</a></sup>的<a href="/wiki/%E7%BA%A4%E7%BB%B4%E7%B4%A0%E9%85%B6" title="纤维素酶">纤维素酶</a>、以及<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%BE%B1%E7%B2%89%E9%85%B6" title="淀粉酶">淀粉酶</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-OlempskaBeer2006_264-0"><a href="#cite_note-OlempskaBeer2006-264">[258]</a></sup>、<a href="/wiki/%E8%94%97%E7%B3%96%E9%85%B6" title="蔗糖酶">蔗糖酶</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E8%9B%8B%E7%99%BD%E9%85%B6" title="蛋白酶">蛋白酶</a>与<a href="/wiki/%E6%9C%A8%E8%81%9A%E7%B3%96%E9%85%B6" title="木聚糖酶">木聚糖酶</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Polizeli2005_265-0"><a href="#cite_note-Polizeli2005-265">[259]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E5.8F.83.E8.A6.8B"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="参见">参见</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;section=44" title="编辑章节：参见">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h2><span id=".E8.A8.BB.E8.85.B3"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="注脚">注脚</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;section=45" title="编辑章节：注脚">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div id="references-NoteFoot"><ol class="references">
<li id="cite_note-79"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-79">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">为旧时分类，因爲是<a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%A6%E7%B3%BB%E7%BE%A4" title="并系群">并系群</a>，现已被分拆成多个不同的门。详见<a href="#分类">#分类</a>一节</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-108"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-108">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">也是旧分类名词，现在已不使用，约等同于现在的<a href="/wiki/%E5%82%98%E8%8F%8C%E7%B6%B1" title="伞菌纲">伞菌纲</a></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-121"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-121">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">部分中文翻译参考 <cite class="citation book">贺新生. <a class="external text" href="http://www.ecsponline.com/goods.php?id=169066" rel="nofollow">现代菌物分类系统</a>. <a href="/wiki/%E7%A7%91%E5%AD%A6%E5%87%BA%E7%89%88%E7%A4%BE" title="科学出版社">科学出版社</a>. 2015 <span class="reference-accessdate"> [<span class="nowrap">2018-07-18</span>]</span>. <a href="/wiki/Special:%E7%BD%91%E7%BB%9C%E4%B9%A6%E6%BA%90/9787030451637" title="Special:网络书源/9787030451637"><span title="国际标准书号">ISBN</span> 9787030451637</a>. （原始内容<a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20210115134207/http://www.ecsponline.com/goods.php?id=169066" rel="nofollow">存档</a>于2021-01-15）.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C&amp;rft.au=%E8%B4%BA%E6%96%B0%E7%94%9F&amp;rft.btitle=%E7%8E%B0%E4%BB%A3%E8%8F%8C%E7%89%A9%E5%88%86%E7%B1%BB%E7%B3%BB%E7%BB%9F&amp;rft.date=2015&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.isbn=9787030451637&amp;rft.pub=%E7%A7%91%E5%AD%B8%E5%87%BA%E7%89%88%E7%A4%BE&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.ecsponline.com%2Fgoods.php%3Fid%3D169066&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-122"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-122">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">此为传统分类中属于Eumycota的类群</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-124"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-124">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%A0%B8%E5%BD%A2%E8%9F%B2" title="核形虫">核形虫</a>与<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Fonticula" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="泉生虫"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%B3%89%E7%94%9F%E8%9F%B2&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="泉生虫（页面不存在）">泉生虫</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fonticula" title="en:Fonticula"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Fonticula</span></a></span>）</span></span>都没有<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%B9%BE%E4%B8%81%E8%B3%AA" title="几丁质">几丁质</a>组成的<a href="/wiki/%E7%B4%B0%E8%83%9E%E5%A3%81" title="细胞壁">细胞壁</a>，具有圆盘状的粒线体皱褶，以<a href="/wiki/%E8%AE%8A%E5%BD%A2%E8%9F%B2" title="变形虫">变形虫</a>的型态生长，以<a href="/wiki/%E5%90%9E%E5%99%AC%E4%BD%9C%E7%94%A8" title="吞噬作用">吞噬作用</a>取得养分，<a href="/wiki/%E5%9F%BA%E5%9B%A0%E7%B5%84" title="基因组">基因组</a>中缺少第二型（Division II）<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="chitin synthetase" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="几丁质合成酶"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%B9%BE%E4%B8%81%E8%B3%AA%E5%90%88%E6%88%90%E9%85%B6&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="几丁质合成酶（页面不存在）">几丁质合成酶</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/chitin_synthetase" title="en:chitin synthetase"><span dir="auto" lang="en">chitin synthetase</span></a></span>）</span></span>的基因，这些特征都与真菌不同。隐真菌门虽然也有许多物种缺乏细胞壁，但它们仍有第二型几丁质合成酶的基因，细胞壁的缺乏可能是该演化支分支以后才丢失的特征<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Tedersoo2018_2-4"><a href="#cite_note-Tedersoo2018-2">[2]</a></sup></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-125"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-125">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">这四个亚门随后在不同研究中，分别被提升至门的地位</span>
</li>
</ol></div>
<h2><span id=".E5.8F.82.E8.80.83.E6.96.87.E7.8C.AE"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="参考文献">参考文献</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;section=46" title="编辑章节：参考文献">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<li><a href="/wiki/%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C%E8%A7%82%E5%AF%9F%E8%80%85" title="真菌观察者">Mushroom Observer</a> (<a class="external text" href="http://mushroomobserver.org" rel="nofollow">mushroomobserver.org</a> （<a class="external text" href="//web.archive.org/web/20210125023330/http://mushroomobserver.org/" rel="nofollow">页面存档备份</a>，存于<a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%92%E8%81%94%E7%BD%91%E6%A1%A3%E6%A1%88%E9%A6%86" title="互联网档案馆">互联网档案馆</a>）), a collaborative fungus recording and identification project</li></ul>
